Utilizing the NEMESIS ID AI engine, investigators successfully followed all of the disbursements downstream to evaluate if there were ANY wallets where funds were recombined. To provide a solid, documented evidentiary trail to use for motions, subpoenas, or warrants, this visualization explicitly details the unredacted wallet address, the transaction ID (hash) for each transfer, the entities involved, and the transaction date. This definitive proof supports immediate seizure/forfeiture motions and allows CALEO to move much faster, drastically increasing the likelihood of recovering victim funds.
